<p style='font:9pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'>Emerging growth company <ix:nonNumeric name='dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany' contextRef='D210708' format='ixt-sec:boolballotbox'>&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></p>
<p style='font:9pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act.[&#160;&#160;&#160;]</p>

<hr style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'/><hr style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'/><p style='line-height:0;margin:0'></p>
<hr style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'/><p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><kbd style='position:absolute;font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-left:0pt'><b>Item 5.03</b></kbd><kbd style='margin-left:63pt'></kbd><span style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'><b>Amendments to Articles of Incorporation or Bylaws; Change in Fiscal Year</b></span><b>.</b>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'>On July 8, 2021, Associated Banc-Corp (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) filed a Certificate regarding its 6.125% Perpetual Preferred Stock, Series&#160;C (the &#8220;Series&#160;C Preferred Stock&#8221;) with the Wisconsin Department of Financial Institutions to eliminate from its Amended and Restated Articles of Incorporation (the &#8220;Articles&#8221;) all matters set forth in the Articles regarding the shares of Series&#160;C Preferred Stock. &#160;All outstanding shares of the Series&#160;C Preferred Stock were redeemed by the Company on June 15, 2021, and the Series C Preferred Stock was delisted from the New York Stock Exchange as of such date. </p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'>The Certificate relating to the Series&#160;C Preferred Stock, which became effective on the date of filing, is attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;3.1 and incorporated herein by reference.</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><kbd style='position:absolute;font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-left:0pt'><b>Item 9.01</b></kbd><kbd style='margin-left:63pt'></kbd><span style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'><b>Financial Statements and Exhibits</b></span><b>.</b>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'>&#160;</p>

<DESCRIPTION>CERTIFICATE RELATING TO THE SERIES C PREFERRED STOCK EFFECTIVE JULY 8, 2021
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<!-- Produced by EDGARsuite software, Advanced Computer Innovations, Inc., Copyright (C) 2008-2020 [PPXS9DHT815PVJYSZXXC]. www.edgarsuite.com -->
<HEAD>
<TITLE>EXHIBIT 3.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY>
<DIV style=margin-left:32pt;width:468pt><P align=right style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><B>EXHIBIT 3.1</B></P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><P align=center style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><B>ASSOCIATED BANC-CORP</B></P>
<P align=center style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><B>CERTIFICATE RELATING TO</B></P>
<P align=center style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><B>THE</B></P>
<P align=center style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><B>SERIES C PREFERRED STOCK</B></P>
<P align=center style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>Pursuant to Section 180.0602</P>
<P align=center style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:24pt'>of the Wisconsin Business Corporation Law</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-indent:36pt'>The undersigned, Associated Banc-Corp, a Wisconsin corporation (the &#8220;Company&#8221;), in accordance with the provisions of Section&#160;180.0602 of Wisconsin Business Corporation Law, for the purposes of eliminating from the Amended and Restated Articles of Incorporation of the Company (the &#8220;Articles&#8221;) all matters set forth in the Articles of Amendment to the Articles regarding the 6.125% Perpetual  Preferred Stock, Series C (the &#8220;Series C Preferred Stock&#8221;) of the Company filed with the Wisconsin Department of Financial Institutions on June 4, 2015 (the &#8220;Articles Amendment&#8221;) with respect to the Series C Preferred Stock, par value $1.00 per share, of the Company for purposes of cancelling the Series C Preferred Stock, hereby certifies that:</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:36pt'>1.</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:63pt></KBD>The undersigned is the duly elected and acting Executive Vice President, General Counsel and Corporate Secretary.&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:36pt'>2.</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:63pt></KBD>In accordance with the provisions of Section&#160;180.0602 of Wisconsin Business Corporation Law, the Board of Directors of the Company has adopted the following resolutions on April 27, 2021 eliminating from the Articles all matters set forth in the Articles Amendment with respect to the Series C Preferred Stock for purposes of cancelling the Series C Preferred Stock:&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:10pt;margin-left:36pt;margin-right:36pt'><A name=_cp_text_2_24 />WHEREAS, pursuant to Sections&#160;180.1002(8) and 180.0602(3)(b)(2) of the Wisconsin Business Corporation Law, the Board may eliminate from the Articles by amendment the provisions thereof related to the shares of Series C Preferred Stock without shareholder approval, provided that no shares of the Series C Preferred Stock are then outstanding.</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:10pt;margin-left:36pt;margin-right:36pt'>NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT RESOLVED, that the officers of the Company be, and each of them hereby is, authorized for and in the name of the Company to take or cause to be taken such actions as are necessary or advisable to effect the elimination from the Articles the provisions thereof related to the shares of Series C Preferred Stock, including, without limitation, the preparation, execution and filing of an appropriate certification and articles of amendment with the Wisconsin Department of Financial Institutions.</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-indent:36pt'>3. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;All outstanding shares of the Series C Preferred Stock were redeemed by the Company as of June 15, 2021. </P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'>The undersigned declares under penalty of perjury under the laws of the State of Wisconsin that the matters set out in the foregoing Certificate are true of his own knowledge and that the </P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><HR style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'><P style=line-height:0;margin:0></P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'>foregoing Certificate has been duly adopted by the Company&#8217;s Board of Directors in accordance with the Wisconsin Business Corporation Law.</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:24pt'>Executed at Milwaukee, Wisconsin, on July 7, 2021.</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-left:216pt'><B>ASSOCIATED BANC-CORP</B></P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;margin-left:216pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:0pt'>By:</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:27pt></KBD><FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'>/s/ Randall J. Erickson&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</FONT>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;margin-left:216pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:0pt'>Name:</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:45pt></KBD>Randall J. Erickson&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:24pt;margin-left:261.35pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-left:-45.35pt'>Title:</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:-0.35pt></KBD>Executive Vice President, General Counsel and Corporate Secretary &nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>Drafted by:</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>Brian D. Anhalt</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>Godfrey &amp; Kahn, S.C.</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>833 E. Michigan Street, Suite 1800</P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:24pt'>Milwaukee, Wisconsin 53202</P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><P align=center style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'>2</P>

var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
